Susanna Moore (she could have been Susanna Case), was Susanna Francis in 1850. Daniel Galusha was born in March 1791 probably in Williamstown, Berkshire Co. , NY Sarah Stetson, daughter of Benjamin and Mary (Johnson) Stetson. Marion, may have been a granddaughter, Marion Blanding. Jeremiah Green was born March 28, 1784 probably in Petersburg, Rensselaer Co.
